by check mark whether the Registrant is an emerging growth company as defined in Rule 405 of the Securities Act of 1933 (&#167;230.405
of this chapter) or Rule 12b-2 of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934 (&#167;240.12b-2 of this chapter).</span></p>

    <div style="page-break-before: always; margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 12pt"><table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; width: 100%"><tr><td style="text-align: center; width: 100%">&#160;</td></tr></table></div>
    <!-- Field: /Page -->



<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.5in"><span style="font-size: 10pt"></span></p>

<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0; width: 100%"><tr style="vertical-align: top; text-align: justify">
<td style="width: 0%"></td><td style="width: 10%; text-align: left"><span style="font-size: 10pt"><b>Item 8.01.</b></span></td><td style="text-align: justify; width: 90%"><span style="font-size: 10pt"><b>Other Events.</b></span></td>
</tr></table>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.5in"><span style="font-size: 10pt">&#160;</span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.5in"><span style="font-size: 10pt">On April 4, 2021 (the &#8220;USD Notes Redemption Date&#8221;), The Coca-Cola
Company (the &#8220;Company&#8221;) redeemed all of the outstanding (i) $1,106,476,000 aggregate principal amount of the Company&#8217;s
3.200% notes due 2023 (the &#8220;3.200% Notes&#8221;) and (ii) $392,055,000 aggregate principal amount of the Company&#8217;s 2.500%
notes due 2023 (the &#8220;2.500% Notes&#8221;), under the Amended and Restated Indenture, dated as of April 26, 1988, as amended by the
First Supplemental Indenture, dated as of February 24, 1992, and the Second Supplemental Indenture, dated as of November 1, 2007 (as so
amended, the &#8220;Indenture&#8221;), between the Company and Deutsche Bank Trust Company Americas, as trustee.</span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.5in"><span style="font-size: 10pt">&#160;</span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.5in"><span style="font-size: 10pt">Subsequently, on April 8, 2021 (the &#8220;Euro Notes Redemption Date&#8221;
and, together with the USD Notes Redemption Date, the &#8220;Redemption Date&#8221;), the Company redeemed all of the outstanding &#8364;867,431,000
aggregate principal amount of the Company&#8217;s 0.750% notes due 2023 (the &#8220;0.750% Notes&#8221; and, together with the 3.200%
Notes and the 2.500% Notes, the &#8220;Notes&#8221;), under the Indenture.</span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.5in"><span style="font-size: 10pt">&#160;</span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.5in"><span style="font-size: 10pt">The Notes were redeemed at a redemption price of 100% of the principal
amount of the applicable Notes, plus accrued and unpaid interest to, but excluding, the applicable Redemption Date plus the applicable
&#8220;make-whole&#8221; premium.</span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.5in"><span style="font-size: 10pt">&#160;</span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"></p>
